Our Family Viewed from the Perspective of Meaning
 You may remember that the teacher mentioned recently that in order to establish an ideal family, men and women must become pure gold, becoming both plus and minus like pure gold.
 The root of human ideals is different.
 Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity, branch out together like a tree. This is similar to an inverted tree. When you look at a tree, it always stands upright, but think about how we humans come down upside down.
 Can you see the roots of the tree? "No." Is it good for the roots of the tree to be exposed? Is it better if they are not exposed? The less visible, the better. Then should God see it or not?
 If you quietly observe the ground, it is all one. When you look at this ground, the soil is the same, but harmony arises from the soil. When you see flowers or trees of various colors and types, it is very miraculous. You see, the quality that makes a red flower a red flower must have existed in the ground. Did it not? Of course, the seed has that quality, but the fact that it absorbs all relative elements to form such a shape means that it is all supplied from the ground.
 When we look at our eyes, Western people have bright blue eyes, and I thought, "Where did that come from?" (Laughter) Such brightness does not appear from the ground. Of course, they inherit traditions from their parents, but the elements that allow them to have blue eyes are absorbed from all relative materials. When we see this, the ground becomes the motivation to cultivate all beings, just as it is the source of our human ideals. If there is an invisible ideal tree, there must be something invisible at the roots of that tree. Do you think that is the case? "Yes."
 Then, who governs this world? It is the idea man, the one with ideals. Isn't that right? That is the truth. Those who have wisdom and good ideas govern the world. It is not power that governs. It is not money that governs. It is not knowledge that governs. What kind of person is an idea man? He is someone who knows how to utilize the power of harmony. It is the same.
 When we look at it this way, we see that humanity has fallen. What is the fall? It is a separation. The roots have separated from the trunk of the tree. Have the trunk and branches separated? "Branches." If the branches have separated, it is not a problem. You can just cut them off. But if the roots have split, will that tree live or die? "It will die." It cannot help but die.
 If you look for yourself as the center, you will ultimately lose everything.
 What is the fall? The roots have changed. The roots. Because of the fall, the roots have become the roots of evil. Do you know that? "Yes." Who is the ancestor of humanity? "Satan." Do you know that Satan is the ancestor of humanity? Is it just words that your ancestor is Satan? Is that the truth? "That is the truth." Really? "Yes."
 If Satan is the ancestor of humanity, what is the first branch of Satan? What could it be? It is the hand. It is our limbs. When you look at it this way, if you have hands, do these hands try to pull everything towards themselves? How do they act? They keep trying to gather everything, right? Ultimately, what is it? It is a struggle to find each other. It is a struggle to possess each other.
 This history has begun. Even now, such history continues. Externally, it seems that all humans are seeking and possessing everything globally, but internally, they do not realize that they are completely losing everything. Today, the world is all like that; the United States is the same. The U.S. tries to move the whole world, but centered on itself, it ends up losing the world instead of finding it.
 Recently, nations have also been losing in this way. The fact that American youth have all become individualistic is a strange sign for a Christian nation. Can that be? How can individualism arise centered on Christian thought? Centered on Christianity, they tried to evangelize the world and do all sorts of things, but in the end, they lost God. Individualism does not believe in God. As a result, even the United States...
 Do you have a country? There is no concept of a nation. They have lost their nation. There is no concept of society either. They have no concept of their parents. There is no concept of siblings. They have even lost the value of humanity, and nowadays, they have lost love, just like animals. They have lost everything. Now they have lost even love. They have lost everything, including love, human value, and even their own lives, which are like those of dogs and animals. Is that true or not? "That is true." Is that what you think? These hands and this head have been trying to possess everything throughout human history, but in the end, they have lost everything. This is the historical reality. This is a harsh fact. Do you understand that?
 When we look at it this way, why have humans come out trying to possess the world centered on themselves? They have never thought about what they would lose. Then, even though they tried to manage absolutely and preserve absolutely, why did they lose? This is the historical problem. If such a phenomenon occurred in a specific region, like Belvedere in the U.S., it could be denied, but the fact that it has occurred globally at the same time is a surprising and significant issue that we cannot overlook. That is an undeniable fact, right? "Yes."
 All beings must have absolute life, thought, and love.
 So, did America want it to be this way? Did the American people want it to be this way? Did the German people or the people of advanced nations want it to be this way? They all did not want it, so why did it happen? Was it because there was no motivation to act beyond the world, or was there motivation? "There was motivation." When we think about this and observe reality, we must recognize that without motivation, without cause, there cannot be a result. That is the scientific way of thinking today.
 Now, what is that motivation? When we see that there is a motivation that causes phenomena contrary to the path of this world, it is a motivation that is different from our human way of thinking. Does it happen just because the American people say so? Can all the thinkers in America say, "World, become this way," and it will happen? "No." Therefore, there is a causal existence greater than the power of any nation or the combined intellect of scholars on this earth that is creating the world in this way. If there is such a substantial existence, what could that existence be? That existence transcends humanity. If such a being exists, it can be called God, a fist, or a shoe; the name does not matter.
 So, how will the future world be? This is a curious question. When we delve into this curious question, we can discover new ideas. We have now entered a stage where trying to possess everything will lead to complete ruin. So, if I say I will give everything instead, what do you think will happen? What do you think? "That's a good idea." Why is it a good idea?
 When we look at the current global reality, where there is hope in the world and hope for humanity, if we draw a conclusion, we must cut off the history of wanting to possess and initiate a movement of giving on a global scale. If a religion or some ideology can emerge that can carry out such a movement, we can think that it will be a way to reform human history and guide it to a new ideal world.
 If there is a God, and if that God is a personal God, then that God must have a way of thinking. What would that way of thinking and ideal be? It must be different from humans. It is the opposite, right? It cannot be anything but the opposite. As a result of humanity's fall, everyone fought to possess centered on themselves and ended up being ruined. Then, what kind of human would a non-fallen human be? It would be 180 degrees different from a fallen human. Do you understand? "Yes."
 God is a good being; we generally think of God as a good being. Whether He is good or not is uncertain, but we think that way anyway. What is Satan? He is evil. Then what is evil and what is good? Who decides that? You must understand this clearly. If you teach this clearly to the individualistic American youth, everything will be resolved.
 What is evil? Evil is self-serving. Absolute self-serving is absolute evil... What is good? It is absolutely serving others. What is absolutely serving oneself? "Absolute evil." What is absolutely serving others? "Absolute good." (Applause) So, what kind of person is a good person? A good person is one who serves others. A person who says, "I don't mind dying if it is for others" is a good person.
 Is life absolute or relative? "Absolute." Then, in such life, how many loves are there? "One absolute love." Do today's American youth say there is one absolute love? These kids! Do they know what that means? It means they are completely clueless! (Laughter) It is the same. What is that? That cannot even be called love. Are there two ideals? "No." Why? Why is it no? It would be good if there were two. Money is better at two hundred dollars than one hundred dollars, right? Why? Is life one, and love two, and ten? "No." Is the ideal one hundred? "No." Which one would you choose? Which one is better? "One." Since it is one life? "One love." Then? "One ideal." Do you all agree? If it is one, that is a wonderful thought. (Laughter)
 So, where will true life arise, and where will true life maintain happiness? All these questions arise from there... It is in the mutual love and mutual giving that ideal love is born. Therefore, when parents mutually wish for each other, wonderful sons and daughters are born. Thus, when absolute life, absolute love, and absolute ideals are possessed to serve all beings, there is a heavenly principle that all beings must stand as relative values. You must understand that there is a principle of heaven.
 The greatest and most powerful force in the world is love.
 Why is that? Because God created all things as His counterpart. Therefore, because God resembles that, all beings cannot help but comply with it; that is a natural conclusion. For this reason, we can conclude that humans can govern the universe. Do you think that is wonderful? "Yes." What is the most precious thing in the universe? Reverend Moon is said to be a millionaire, and people make a fuss about Reverend Moon, but that is all nonsense. However, if one possesses absolute life, love, and ideals, they can transcend borders, nations, races, and history. Therefore, any being that seeks truth must comply with this heavenly principle, which is why even if a person like Reverend Moon comes here to America and tells you to do this or that, you do not complain and move. Why is that? Do you think that could be the case? "Yes."
 You all, why did you come here instead of going to American churches in the morning? There are many excellent theologians, professors, and doctors who speak English well; why did you come here? You could be sitting comfortably in a warm place, listening like this. What are you doing here? Why did you come, you guys? Why did you come? Even if you are insulted and hit, you still like it. Do you know why? It is the same principle as what I said earlier. You must understand that this formula applies across time and space. Do you think that could be the case? "Yes." If that is not the case, then everything the teacher says is a blatant lie. A blatant lie.
 What is the greatest and most powerful force in this world? It is the pursuit of the one and only life. It is the pursuit of the one and only love. It is the pursuit of the one and only thought. You must understand that there is no greater power than that. Do you think that could be the case? "Yes." It seems so, right? "Yes." Even God cannot stop that. God cannot stop it. God must follow that law.
 Do you think God is weak against love? Is He strong? "He is weak." Would God say, "I absolutely do not need love, you love"? God cannot move in the face of love. You must understand that if there is love, everything else before God seems to disappear.
Moon is a strong person in love. Is he a weak person? "He is a weak person." Reverend Moon also says he doesn't need love; he says Reverend Moon is also helpless in love? What is it like? It's the same, the same. So, how close is God to me? With love, God becomes my friend, and even if I am underfoot, He remains still. Even if I ride on Him and dance, He remains still. What kind of power can allow that? It cannot be done with life or with thought. Only love is possible, only love. What kind of love is it? Is it love that is for me, or love that is for others? "Love that is for others." Now, I understand this. If there is someone with such essence, then now I can conclude the whole. There is no way to cut that connection. God cannot cut it either. Since God cannot cut it, there is no need to mention Satan. He cannot even come close. He cannot even come close.

Now, the Unification Church and Reverend Moon are all braking for you. The world is saying, "You cannot go." After that, America pulls back saying, "You cannot go," and some religions say, "You cannot go," and everyone says, "You cannot go." Can they stop it? "No." If it is true, they can stop it. If it is the power of love, they can stop it. Why? Because Reverend Moon knows God's love, I am doing this play.

If you put your life on the line for others, the ideal world will come in an instant. Now, an hour has already passed, and while talking, it seems like only ten minutes have gone by, right? "Yes." This morning, there was not a single person dozing off. Why is that? Because when we talk about love, everyone likes it. (Applause) Now, you all understand, right? Looking at the world, it is undeniable. If the world is not like that, it will perish. All of it.

Now, if God truly blesses such a person and truly loves such a person..., from this moment, if the 4 billion people of the world throw away all the traditions and habits of history and start saying "This land," and become people who care for others, what will happen? Will God remain still? Will God be happy and want to love? God will shout, dance, sing, and do all sorts of things.

Do you think the ideal world will come? Do you think the ideal world will all come? "Yes." You know it, but is that ideal world far away? Is it close? "It is close." If 4 billion people turn around at once and say "This land," it will all happen, they say. It is just a matter of turning around. Will it take an instant? Will it take decades? "An instant." How is it? It will happen in an instant. If you just turn your heart, if you just turn your direction, it will be done.

So how should this be turned? When you know that it is beneficial without loss, you will turn even if you are told not to. Do you think that will happen? "Yes." Then, has heaven come closer to you or further away? "It has come closer." So, you must understand that Jesus also said, "The kingdom of heaven is near." Did he say the kingdom is in heaven or in your hearts? "In the heart."

Then how can you know whether the kingdom of heaven exists or not? You can know by seeing if you have become a person of the kingdom of heaven. Who is that person of the kingdom? It is a person like God. What kind of person is a person like God? It is a person who is willing to give their life for the world. It is a person who wants to love the world. It is a person who says that there must be one unity centered on God. What kind of doctrine is that? That is ideal religiousism, and the representative of that ideal religiousism is Jesusism. What is that Jesusism? It is Godism.

So, Jesus said, "I did not come to the world to be served." "No." What is "no," you rascal! (Laughter) How did he say it? "No." What is "no," right? "No!" (Laughter) This is something even the teacher cannot do. God cannot do it either. If you say "no," neither God nor the teacher can do it. That is why, with the truth, God can be made to submit. From the position of knowing the truth, you can attack even God. Anyone can attack anyone.

When Jesus was carrying the cross, did he say, "Kill those Roman soldiers, my twelve disciples! If Christianity develops globally later, take revenge"? Did he bless them? He blessed them. What kind of doctrine is that? That is the doctrine that will conquer the world. It is the doctrine that will establish heaven in the human world, the doctrine that will establish the ideal world. Jesus knew this thought, knew this doctrine and truth, and knew that ideal, which is why he made such claims.

What about Christians? Are there people who like Christians these days? Is that so? They are proud and only think of themselves. "We alone will go to heaven, and you will face judgment at the end." They are saying such nonsense. (Laughter) Because Christians only thought of that, they became individualistic. Have you thought about why individualism became so? The Christians who are said to be good, when they meet, they all say they dislike it, and when they meet a Unification Church member who is said to be bad, they all say they like it; this contradictory phenomenon has occurred. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Why is that? It is because they are different. They are trying to care for the whole and care for people, so all these Unification Church members... If they can catch those people, they can gain benefits... Now you understand, right? You got it? "Yes."

You will say, "Let's go with American youth centered on ourselves, centered on individualism." Will you say, "Oh, I dislike individualism; I will sacrifice for the whole"? What will it be? "Second." What will it be? You rascals, what is it? "Second." First? "No." You like the first, right? "No." No, no, no! "No good." (Laughter) Now you understand? "Yes." "Ah, what I am doing is to please our teacher, to let our teacher know," will you do that, "If the teacher knows, I will give, if not, I will do it alone"? Will you do that? "Second." First? "No." No, yes? "No." (Laughter)

Some people say, "Oh, the teacher said that if I do this for three years, he will let me marry, bless me, so I am selling peanuts and doing evangelism for my marriage." Did that work? "No." When you go to the marriage ceremony, will you say, "Oh, wedding march and whatnot, now I have graduated. Oh, how nice!" Will you say, "Let's go again!"? (Laughter) What will you do? You are answering but turning your eyes over there, trying not to see me. (Laughter) Answer clearly. What will it be? "Second." You clearly answered me. I will not forget that. (Laughter) Do you understand? "Yes."

"Hey! That person is an idealist, a wonderful person," when they say that, is he well-dressed, or is he wearing shabby clothes but caring for others? What is an idealist? "Second." Some people cannot sleep at night and walk around dozing during the day. Is that the ideal man? "Yes." (Laughter) You want to get such a husband and such a wife, you rascals? "Yes." Is that so? "Yes." You cannot help but say yes, right? "No." Your eyes are smiling, but your mouth is crying. (Laughter) Sorry, but even regarding our mother, I know that she does not like it when I take her around, but what do you think? (Laughter) Shouldn't mothers be like that, or should they not? (Laughter) You all know. It seems you all know. (Laughter)

The history until now has been a history of finding a family centered on one person. Now, the title today is "Our Family Viewed from the Will." So, what has God been doing until now? If Reverend Moon teaches so simply, everyone should understand, but until now, even looking at the Bible, they do not know that. They all do not know whether it is bean porridge or red bean porridge. However, you must understand that God Himself cannot do anything until such a person is raised.

In leading human history, where is the destination that God is trying to settle? Before making the world such a base, He is searching for one individual centered on one family. That is it. Therefore, the conclusion is that He must send such a man by creating another root. However, since that has failed, He reaches the conclusion that He must find a man or woman who can do more than that.

So, what kind of man and woman is that? It is a person who will give for heaven and earth, who will give for the spirit world, and who will give for this world today, and who will say, "I will go for eternity until I reach that." Such a person is the Messiah, the Messiah. Do you understand? Because they know that to receive completely, one must give completely, they know that if they give completely, they will receive completely... Therefore, if you look at the history of Israel until now, it is all a history of finding one person, a history of finding one family.

What kind of work did they make that one person do? They made him do things that the world opposes, things that are contrary to the world. They have been made to do such opposing acts. Even looking at the family of Adam, Cain and Abel, Abel was trying to return to God by sacrificing even his life. How wonderful would it have been if Abel had blessed his brother? Then how quickly would God's will have been fulfilled?

Look. Noah also faced opposition for 120 years. To build a boat, he should have built it by the river, but he built it on the top of Mount Ararat. So they said he was crazy. Would you believe that? Would you believe it if your father did that? If you were Noah's son, would you believe it? Is there even one person who would believe it? There is not a single person. If there is not one person, then one person is needed. Did God make him do opposing work or not? He made him do opposing work, right? He made him do all opposing work.

Look again. Even though Abraham was the son of an idol merchant, God commanded him to leave everything behind and flee from Ur of the Chaldeans. When God said, "Hey, Abraham! Your descendants will flourish like the stars of heaven and like the grains of sand on the earth. So listen to my words and leave everything and go," would he have consulted his mother and father? Would he have consulted his brothers? If he had consulted, he could not go. He was like a gypsy, a gypsy. He often slept under some small tree, often begging for food. Would there be anyone who would prepare a feast and invite him? There would be no one, so he went all the way to the land of Egypt, a foreign land. Did he go there because he could live and there was a good settlement? He went there and lost his wife to Pharaoh and his nephew was taken, and he ended up in a situation where he could die in prison.

But did Abraham blame God? Even in the midst of prison, did he believe that what God had blessed him with would come true, standing in such a lonely place? (Laughter) That is for the sake of finding one person, just one person. Abraham was a person who passed that test. When facing Pharaoh, Pharaoh could change a hundred times, but Abraham, even if pushed a thousand times, would not change his position, so heaven reached out and finally cooperated with Abraham. Even if God cooperates, Satan cannot accuse him because there is no one like Abraham.

Moses was the same. He was single-minded in wanting to help his country, and even if he faced death, his determined heart did not change.

Now, what about John the Baptist? Did he change or not? "He changed." John the Baptist became a monster who caused Israel to perish and ruined history. That is why Christianity has become like this. Then did Jesus change or not? "He did not change." In the end, when he was going to the cross, even knowing that God had forsaken him, he still held onto God, saying, "My God! Why have you forsaken me?" What about you? "I do not change." It is easy for you to answer. But do you know how difficult it is to act like that? What about Peter? What about you? Because Jesus died without changing, and because heaven is alive, he resurrected that Jesus and conquered the world.

What about our Unification Church, Reverend Moon? "He does not change." How do you believe that? Who knows if I am a global con artist? The world says so, right? "No." Because you believe that, you are crazy. It is because you are crazy that it is so. You are under hypnosis and have been brainwashed, right?

"No."

Satan says to God, "Can Reverend Moon take responsibility for the world or not? I cannot believe that your son, Reverend Moon, can take responsibility for the world." Then God will say, "He can." Then Satan will say, "Let's see if he can be shaken by a global attack. Let's see if he falls down and retreats." The whole world... Therefore, he must stand in a lonely position that no one else can take while facing opposition globally, and even if attacked, he must hold onto God... You must understand that God waits until Satan, who was accusing the world, retreats.

In human history, there is no one other than Reverend Moon who is causing global events and receiving global attacks without dying in this world. That is a fact. Is that right? "Yes." So, people of all races are in one place, facing attacks from all races of the world. That is unprecedented.

When you are truly genuine, God's power comes even if you do not want it to come. How good is that? "Absolutely." It is absolutely good. Therefore, the absolute God also likes that.

So, Reverend Moon is a heretic. What is it? "No." Then what is it? "True parents." Do you know the foundation of that? Everything that is not like that is fake. The time when the fake calls the genuine fake is the end of that time.

Is your pure gold fake or real? "Real." Then what are you? "Genuine." What is genuine? Why is pure gold good? When electricity passes through, pure gold has no resistance. It is one hundred percent. What is that? It is all '
"Come in! Hurry up and come in!" Because of this... The power to do so is what makes it real. It's an invitation to come in. Is that the same for you all? If the water has come in, where does it go? It doesn't just disappear; it circulates. But because it can't do that, the path is blocked here, so it can't happen. That's why there's no need to say to God, "Please recognize me." If I am pure gold, even if I say, "Don't come, God," His power will still come. Even if I ask, "God, please teach me," He won't teach me. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Have you become that kind of man? "Yes."

When gold is placed in a crucible and the king commands, "Melt, you gold!" it melts, right? If gold is placed in the crucible and the king says, "Hey, I am the king of this country. So melt!" does it melt? "No." If he says, "Let the light turn black," does it turn black? "No." Can it receive punishment just because the king says, "You didn't listen to me, so you will be punished"? Does it get punished? "No." What does this mean? It means that the real thing has a value that is beyond hell and does not need interference; it cannot be interfered with. God cannot enter my dominion unless He is like me, and the king cannot enter my dominion unless he is like me; this is the authority I have. Do you understand that? "Yes."

That's why it doesn't matter who recognizes me... What does it matter if God recognizes me? What does it matter if the king recognizes me? My authority is better than being recognized by others. Then why should I care for others? This is the problem. Why should I care for others? The one who cares becomes the master, the owner. The one who cares becomes the subject, the subject. Why? Because they resemble God. The one who cannot care cannot possess anything. They are lonely; that's the truth. Isn't it the same for the members of the Unification Church? They just curse every day. If they were told to only care for the teacher, would they all run away? It's the same.

To expand ownership, relative conditions are necessary. If there is one person who dominates the world, no matter how high he is, even if he is the son of God, being alone... Even if he is on the path that connects heaven to hell, that is useless. He will fall. If there is only one, it will fall.

Then what is the ideal of having one? What is the ideal? Is this (pointing while speaking) the ideal? "No." Is this the ideal? "No." What is the ideal? Between this and this, and this and that, which is the ideal? Why is that the ideal? The force that reaches here can also go there, and it acts here, and it acts everywhere; there is no place it does not act. Is the action of force here different from the action of force there? The counterparts here and there are all the same.

So what is the ideal? One here, one there; did the human structure know this at its toes, or not? Does it know even to the hair? (Laughs) How does it know? Because it is completely alive and completely exchanging. When this (pointing while speaking) acts here, it must connect to the whole; it must not be disconnected. That is the ideal. If this happens, what happens? It turns. If it turns, what happens? It goes on forever. You all, if the wheels of a car are straight, what happens? If they are straight? (Laughs) Because the wheels of a car are round, it goes on forever.

There is one man and one woman. Then what should the man and woman do? If the man is alone, what is the ideal? Ultimately, he seeks this (the woman). Therefore, you all have the duty to become one with two. It is all structured that way. There is body and mind, right? They must become one. Similarly, we humans must also become one (mind and body).

This is (pointing while speaking) a nation. Then what happens? This expands step by step. What was narrow becomes wider and wider. It expands from this range. Therefore, to create one, you must create one family. To do this, ultimately, what is it? The man must become one with the woman. This is how the relative relationship gradually expands. How about you? Do you understand what I mean? Individual, family, tribe, nation; ultimately, it moves toward the horizon.

Now, individualism is this kind of principle, this kind of principle. Ownership is this. Then this expands. As ownership increases, everything here becomes mine. (Pointing to what was written) Do you understand what I mean? Then what must be done? I must absorb this. I must keep absorbing. This is how I rise. And while doing so, I expand my sphere of influence.

You must understand why you need relative conditions. Why? To expand ownership. Ownership. Don't you all want to have ownership? "Yes." Seeing that, all the mothers who had tried to elevate their daughters were completely thwarted. They reflected, "Oh, I thought being blessed would be so good, but it ruined everything... It would have been better not to stand in that position!" Do you understand what I mean?

By doing so, the biggest issue became the mothers... Because of that, the environment was half broken. By treating Grandma Hong that way, those mothers felt sympathy. "Wow, did the teacher have such a side? He is a cold and ruthless person," they all began to feel sympathy. That is how it should be. Do you understand? The mothers cannot do that kind of work. I have to do it. Then, what did I do regarding the mothers? For three years, they absolutely could not act freely. They could not even enter the teacher's room freely. For a year, they lived outside, not in a warm place. They were made to live in someone else's house, being told to rent a room in someone else's home.

After doing that for a year, those who were candidates for marriage naturally thought, "Oh, I thought it would be good to be the teacher's partner, but what is this!" That was the strategy. So, as this continued... During that time, the grandmother should not have said anything bad about the teacher. The mother herself should not have said that the teacher was wrong. It was impossible. Without that, if you cannot encompass the emotional Cain, there is no place for the emotional Abel. This is the principle. To become the emotional Abel, one must digest and revive the entire foundation of the emotional Cain. That is the principle. Since the mother cannot do that, the teacher must do it.

Starting from the lowest position, one must inherit the highest glorious throne. 

So, the mother must go through the emotional world, that emotional cross, and the restoration process. For seven years, through this worldwide indemnity course... The teacher laid the victorious foundation, but the mother could not lay it, so she must prepare the way to be able to stand confidently as the central woman of heaven.

That is why during those seven years, as an individual, she fought for three years personally, and then for four years fought for the family, and came this far. 

During that time, how many people followed? From the grandmothers, all the Unification Church members said, "How is the mother? What about taking another mother?" There were all sorts of rumors. If you oppose here, both sides will break apart. You must go silently. You must go without speaking. So, just think about how shocking that must have been. Now you understand what I mean, right?

For example, even the fact that the teacher shares the same birthday led to all sorts of rumors like "He did all this to match the fortune-telling." 

Because they went through such an environment, everyone thinks he is truly impressive. The standard is becoming clearer that "It could not have happened without that person." Some women opposed the mother, saying, "She took the teacher who could have been my husband." There were all sorts of incidents. Do you understand what that means? Even elderly people in their 70s would say, "If I marry the teacher, I will have a dozen children." There were many such things. Those people also hated the mother at one time; they all hated her. Those who hated her all fell away and passed on. That is the principle. Because the teacher understood the principle, he was able to sift through all of this. 

It was an environment where a big fight could break out and everything could turn chaotic. People who have spiritually and emotionally experienced love... In the world, it would have been a situation where lives were at stake. It was a situation where people were saying, "I will kill you, and you will kill me." Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Even though they came as the owners of their emotions and as pioneers of their emotions, they must overcome this emotional cross more than anyone else to become the emotional owners.

So, the mother could not fulfill her role as a mother. To align with that path... I am not teaching or telling you anything. I am saying this for the first time today. I only recently started to care for Grandma Hong. Now, I think I must treat her better than any other grandmother. Now that we have crossed a global hurdle, having come to America, we are no longer bound by conditions. If the mother had not laid that standard, all the children would be affected. It would all become a problem. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." The restoration history is that difficult. You all know nothing.

So, as the standard of the heart expands, the world of the complete center will unfold, and the environment will develop into a complete counterpart. If you establish such a heart-centered standard, evangelism will naturally happen. The mother and grandmother started from the very lowest position. They started from the lowest position in the Unification Church, a position that no one else was treated like. From such a low position, one must inherit the blessing to occupy the throne of the highest glory, so that blessing can last forever. That is how it lasts forever. Do you understand what I mean? I came out that way, I treated our mother that way, and our children also came out that way. I cannot just pass over this principle regarding you. If this could just be passed over, I would not have made our mother do that, and our family would not have engaged in such activities.

But how about you... Can you complain about that? "No." If you complain about the mother, everything will break apart. Everything will break apart. Just wait and see. Those who lived centered on themselves and complained have all fallen away. They all fell away. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Those who think centered on themselves will all break apart. That is the principle, the principle.

You must not be swayed in any environment and must go out earnestly. 

The other day, I quietly observed that the theology students were all placed in positions, and I thought, "The theology students will become our regional leaders, so what is there for us to work hard for?" They had that mindset and ended up in that posture... After the presentation, I was quite worried, and indeed, there have been several weeks like that. Many people have that mindset. Also, since it was said that all the executives would be moved until June, everyone was like, "Oh..." The more that happens, the more they should work harder, and the more they should think about sacrificing themselves, but if they think, "What will happen to me?" they will be eliminated in the future. That is not in accordance with the principle. I know that many members have been like that during that time.

So, when we went out fishing this time, I thought, "Let's see how many of these guys can endure! There will be many who will run away because they dislike it." In the end, I was the only one left. Even Daikang said, "I would like to do this, but let's stop now." He said, "It would be good to stop." Everyone turned back. This time, when I told the tall Gehart, "Hey, let’s go in without clothes!" he was the first to go in and come out. He went in once and came out... (Laughs) Seeing the teacher's expression, it seemed like he wouldn't do it. Also, yesterday, it took three hours to set the net. Now it is a record. It was so tangled... I think that was how your hearts were. Originally, it should have been set within 30 minutes. But I did it all while untangling it. The hardest part was preparing for a bathroom break... I had to go, but there was no place to do it... That was the biggest internal hardship. (Laughs) While doing that, since the teacher did it that way, we caught fish and everything was resolved. Now, if we want to do it again, we have the heart to say, "Yes." That is emotional restoration.

In fact, when I hold a meeting, I know that from the first moment, only curses come out of you. I think, "These kids..." Knowing this situation makes me want to swallow it whole... May is a good month, especially May 3rd, with the 18th wedding anniversary celebration, so I thought it would not do to start like this, and I must know that I am dragging you around here and there.

So, this morning, after listening to your mothers and hearing the teacher's words, you probably learned for the first time that there were such twists behind the teacher's family. Therefore, you must understand that the teacher is someone who does not forgive. You must understand that he is someone who does not know how to forgive. Listening to him, it seems like he lived according to the principle, doesn’t it? "He lived according to the principle."

That is why he can confidently speak before heaven and earth. He is confident. So, as 1976 came to an end, the mother was completely liberated. She was completely liberated. And the teacher too... You must know that the time when the teacher and mother were completely liberated was in 1976.

In that sense, on February 23, 1977, the teacher's birthday, a new era of a new dimension was opened. Do you understand what that means? That is not about the Unification Church. It is about the path the teacher is taking. It is a proclamation about the path the teacher and mother are taking.

Until now, even if the mother spent $10, she reported it to the teacher... I did not allow her to spend freely. However, from now on, I will also give her freedom regarding that. Also, although I am in the overall subjective position, I plan to entrust the mother with household matters and many things in the future. What is special about the mother is that her intuition is quick. Once she thinks someone is "good," that person also thinks she is good. She has a natural talent to discern that. And she is determined to do whatever the teacher asks, and she comes out without losing that determination, which is why she was able to overcome that path of suffering. This corresponds to the patience centered on the purpose.

And what I appreciate about the mother is her character that is willing to give her precious things to you without hesitation, not just to her own children. I see that character as a gift from God. You will be like that.

Western people might think, "Oh, Reverend Moon's wife must have a lot of clothes and treasures," but that is not true. If the mother has something she likes, she tries to share it all with the family. In fact, just the other day, she had to go out but had nothing to wear... There are many times like that. It is not acceptable to think only of oneself and what is good for oneself.

So, what is the first thing? It is to be grateful for the quick intuition and, second, to be grateful for the absolute obedience to the purpose, and third, to give what is not just one's own but the world's without hesitation... A person who is so naturally generous that God cannot help but worry about them has the character of a mother. So, now that I think about it, I feel that all the children we have been given in our family are all blessings from God.

Become a person who follows the principles. 

So now, it has become a matter of nation against nation. Reverend Moon has now gone beyond the standard of being the leader of a single nation. In the future, I believe unimaginable things will happen. Do you understand what that means? "Yes."

That is why you must not think centered on yourselves. If the mother had thought centered on herself, she would not have been able to stay in the Unification Church. She would have already packed her bags and left. Many of your leaders who are self-centered will also pack their bags and retreat. That is how the teacher sees it. Moreover, that is how he is leading. In that respect, he is closely observing how each leader is doing. Those who are self-centered will have issues. You must understand that the teacher's personnel decisions are made based on that principle. You must know that they are made based on the principles. Absolutely... This time, even in Korea, when someone suggested to the teacher, "Oh, what is the need for name value in diplomacy...," I told them to drop it. I absolutely dislike such people. I think, "If you can't do it, I will do it." Such people do not understand the principle. Such people have no emotional foundation. They will automatically collapse. 

To try to establish an emotional standard from a high position... The principle is that the emotional standard rises from the low to the high, but to try to establish an emotional standard from a high position is already akin to Satan.

And I absolutely dislike self-promotion. Mr. Kwak is here now, but you must respect Mr. Kwak a lot. You must recognize that he is a quite representative person in that respect as a higher family. Even here, he does not show off, just going about as if he is not there, but he is doing everything he needs to do. If it is the teacher's command, he will do anything. So now, from the principle research group to the professor academy, he has laid the foundation to be able to take responsibility for anything. Knowing that, it will be fine to respect him in the future. So, all the main points of the principle writing were given to Mr. Kwak. Even when he gives a lecture on the principle, he does not do it centered on himself. He tries to give a principled lecture. And in the future, when the teacher gives a command in the right direction, there are many times when it will be suddenly overturned to the extreme left. How do you...
Is it possible? When people who lived in the Arctic are wearing winter clothes and then go to the equator, they suddenly have to change into summer clothes... Even though they are wearing winter clothes now, if they have to go live at the equator, they must take them off without hesitation. They should be able to take them off without any regrets. I think this incident (anecdote) is a really good opportunity. All of that is the responsibility of Koreans... But the Japanese are the ones who are taking responsibility and handling everything. Isn't that astonishing? Do you understand what I mean? High families, what, the Japanese come and do all this, and they have sullied themselves. Who would oppose that? 'This person is like this, and that person will be like that,' and it turns out exactly as the teacher thought.

Just the other day, it was an event that happened within a week, the association president said he wanted to create a new school, and he would be the principal and do everything like this, which made me feel bad. He said he would be the principal, and who would be what, and he would do this and that, so I told him to drop it. I outright refused. If he had appointed someone below him as the principal, I could understand. This kid, who do you think you are! He is someone who knows better than anyone that a school is needed. Then the other day, he came pleading... 'This absolutely must be done. I will do it out of my own pocket, so please do it.' So then I ordered him to drop everything and said, who would be the principal, and who would do what. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes," the teacher teaches principles, so he does it that way.

So, you all should know this... 'Ah, I also have to do something,' I think today it has become clear. That’s why I see that the mother is ultimately a successful woman as a mother. Moreover, the teacher who created such a woman is also a successful man. (Applause)
